2025-12-01 00:28:40,480 - consoul.tui.app - DEBUG - [TOOL_FLOW] Response check: has_content=**Consoul  AIPowered Terminal Assistant**

Consoul brings conversational AI directly into the command line.
You can chat with Claude, GPT4, Gemini, or local models, either through a fullfeatured terminal UI, a lightweight CLI, or via a Python SDK.

---

### Quick Start
```bash
pip install consoul
export ANTHROPIC_API_KEY=   # or OPENAI_API_KEY / GOOGLE_API_KEY
consoul              # launch the TUI
# or
consoul chat "Explain Python decorators"
```

The SDK example:
```python
from consoul import Consoul
console = Consoul()
print(console.chat("What is 2+2?"))
```

---

### Features

| Category | Highlights |
|----------|------------|
| **Beautiful TUI** | Textualpowered, multiturn, streaming, history search, file attachments, image analysis, themes, mouse/keyboard nav. |
| **MultiProvider** | Claude, GPT4o, Gemini, Ollama (local), LlamaCpp. |
| **AIPowered Tools** | File creation/modification, code search, image analysis, bash execution, web search, URL fetch. |
| **CLI** | `consoul chat`, `consoul ask`, `consoul chat --attach file`. |
| **SDK** | Full toolset, stateful conversations, token/cost metrics. |

---

### Documentation
Full docs at <https://consoul.goatbytes.io>
Quick start guide, configuration, UI, tools, and SDK sections are all covered.

---

### Configuration
Create `~/.consoul/config.yaml`. Example:

```yaml
profiles:
  default:
    model:
      provider: anthropic
      model: claude-3-5-sonnet-20241022
      temperature: 0.7
    tools:
      enabled: true
      permission_policy: balanced
    conversation:
      save_history: true
      max_history: 50
  local:
    model:
      provider: ollama
      model: llama3.2:latest
```

Switch profiles: `consoul --profile local`.

---

### Security
- Permission policies (PARANOID, BALANCED, TRUSTING, UNRESTRICTED)
- Interactive approval for risky ops
- Audit logging
- Command validation

See `SECURITY.md` for details.
